%!TEX root = std.tex
\rSec0[algorithms]{Algorithms library}

\rSec1[algorithms.general]{General}

\pnum
This Clause describes components that \Cpp{} programs may use to perform
algorithmic operations on containers\cxxref{containers} and other sequences.

\pnum
The following subclauses describe components for
non-modifying sequence operations,
mutating sequence operations,
sorting and related operations,
and algorithms from the ISO C library,
as summarized in \tref{algorithms.summary}.

\begin{libsumtab}{Algorithms library summary}{tab:algorithms.summary}
\ref{alg.nonmodifying} & Non-modifying sequence operations  &           \\
\ref{alg.modifying.operations} & Mutating sequence operations & \tcode{<algorithm>} \\
\ref{alg.sorting} & Sorting and related operations      &           \\ \hline
\ref{alg.c.library} & C library algorithms          & \tcode{<cstdlib>} \\ \hline
\end{libsumtab}

\rSec1[algorithm.syn]{Header \tcode{<algorithm>} synopsis}
\indexhdr{algorithm}%

\begin{codeblock}
#include <initializer_list>

namespace std {
  // \ref{alg.nonmodifying}, non-modifying sequence operations
  // \ref{alg.all_of}, all of
  template<class InputIterator, class Predicate>
    constexpr bool all_of(InputIterator first, InputIterator last, Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Predicate>
    bool all_of(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last, Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{bool all_of(I first, S last, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{bool all_of(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.any_of}, any of
  template<class InputIterator, class Predicate>
    constexpr bool any_of(InputIterator first, InputIterator last, Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Predicate>
    bool any_of(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last, Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{bool any_of(I first, S last, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{bool any_of(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.none_of}, none of
  template<class InputIterator, class Predicate>
    constexpr bool none_of(InputIterator first, InputIterator last, Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Predicate>
    bool none_of(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                 ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last, Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{bool none_of(I first, S last, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{bool none_of(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.foreach}, for each
  template<class InputIterator, class Function>
    constexpr Function for_each(InputIterator first, InputIterator last, Function f);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Function>
    void for_each(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                  ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last, Function f);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryInvocable<projected<I, Proj>{}> Fun>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::fun(Fun)>}@
        @\added{for_each(I first, S last, Fun f, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryInvocable<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Fun>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::fun(Fun)>}@
        @\added{for_each(Rng\&\& rng, Fun f, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class InputIterator, class Size, class Function>
    constexpr InputIterator for_each_n(InputIterator first, Size n, Function f);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Size, class Function>
    ForwardIterator for_each_n(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                               ForwardIterator first, Size n, Function f);

  // \ref{alg.find}, find
  template<class InputIterator, class T>
    constexpr InputIterator find(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                                 const T& value);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class T>
    ForwardIterator find(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                         ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                         const T& value);
  template<class InputIterator, class Predicate>
    constexpr InputIterator find_if(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                                    Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Predicate>
    ForwardIterator find_if(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                            ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                            Predicate pred);
  template<class InputIterator, class Predicate>
    constexpr InputIterator find_if_not(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                                        Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Predicate>
    ForwardIterator find_if_not(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                                ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                                Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<I, Proj>, const T*>}@
      @\added{I find(I first, S last, const T\& value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class T, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>, const T*>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{find(Rng\&\& rng, const T\& value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{I find_if(I first, S last, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{find_if(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{I find_if_not(I first, S last, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{find_if_not(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.find.end}, find end
  template<class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    constexpr ForwardIterator1
      find_end(ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2);
  template<class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr ForwardIterator1
      find_end(ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2,
               BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    ForwardIterator1
      find_end(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1,
           class ForwardIterator2, class BinaryPredicate>
    ForwardIterator1
      find_end(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2,
               BinaryPredicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, ForwardIterator I2,}@
        @\added{Sentinel<I2> S2, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<I2, projected<I1, Proj>{}> Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{I1}@
        @\added{find_end(I1 first1, S1 last1, I2 first2, S2 last2,}@
                @\added{Pred pred = Pred\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng1, ForwardRange Rng2, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<iterator_t<Rng2>,}@
          @\added{projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng1>}@
        @\added{find_end(Rng1\&\& rng1, Rng2\&\& rng2, Pred pred = Pred\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.find.first.of}, find first
  template<class InputIterator, class ForwardIterator>
    constexpr InputIterator
      find_first_of(InputIterator first1, InputIterator last1,
                    ForwardIterator first2, ForwardIterator last2);
  template<class InputIterator, class ForwardIterator, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr InputIterator
      find_first_of(InputIterator first1, InputIterator last1,
                    ForwardIterator first2, ForwardIterator last2,
                    BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    ForwardIterator1
      find_first_of(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                    ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
                    ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1,
           class ForwardIterator2, class BinaryPredicate>
    ForwardIterator1
      find_first_of(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                    ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
                    ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2,
                    BinaryPredicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, ForwardIterator I2, Sentinel<I2> S2,}@
        @\added{class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<projected<I1, Proj1>, projected<I2, Proj2>{}> Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{I1}@
        @\added{find_first_of(I1 first1, S1 last1, I2 first2, S2 last2,}@
                      @\added{Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                      @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng1, ForwardRange Rng2, class Proj1 = identity,}@
        @\added{class Proj2 = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<projected<iterator_t<Rng1>, Proj1>,}@
          @\added{projected<iterator_t<Rng2>, Proj2>{}> Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng1>}@
        @\added{find_first_of(Rng1\&\& rng1, Rng2\&\& rng2,}@
                      @\added{Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                      @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.adjacent.find}, adjacent find
  template<class ForwardIterator>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      adjacent_find(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last);
  template<class ForwardIterator, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      adjacent_find(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                    BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator>
    ForwardIterator
      adjacent_find(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                    ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class BinaryPredicate>
    ForwardIterator
      adjacent_find(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                    ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                    BinaryPredicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{I adjacent_find(I first, S last, Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                      @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{adjacent_find(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred = Pred\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.count}, count
  template<class InputIterator, class T>
    constexpr typename iterator_traits<InputIterator>::difference_type
      count(InputIterator first, InputIterator last, const T& value);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class T>
    typename iterator_traits<ForwardIterator>::difference_type
      count(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
            ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last, const T& value);
  template<class InputIterator, class Predicate>
    constexpr typename iterator_traits<InputIterator>::difference_type
      count_if(InputIterator first, InputIterator last, Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Predicate>
    typename iterator_traits<ForwardIterator>::difference_type
      count_if(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last, Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<I, Proj>, const T*>}@
      @\added{iter_difference_t<I>}@
        @\added{count(I first, S last, const T\& value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class T, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>, const T*>}@
      @\added{iter_difference_t<iterator_t<Rng>{}>}@
        @\added{count(Rng\&\& rng, const T\& value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{iter_difference_t<I>}@
        @\added{count_if(I first, S last, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{iter_difference_t<iterator_t<Rng>{}>}@
        @\added{count_if(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{mismatch}, mismatch
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2>
    constexpr pair<InputIterator1, InputIterator2>
      mismatch(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
               InputIterator2 first2);
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr pair<InputIterator1, InputIterator2>
      mismatch(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
               InputIterator2 first2, BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2>
    constexpr pair<InputIterator1, InputIterator2>
      mismatch(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
               InputIterator2 first2, InputIterator2 last2);
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr pair<InputIterator1, InputIterator2>
      mismatch(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
               InputIterator2 first2, InputIterator2 last2,
               BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    pair<ForwardIterator1, ForwardIterator2>
      mismatch(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class BinaryPredicate>
    pair<ForwardIterator1, ForwardIterator2>
      mismatch(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2, BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    pair<ForwardIterator1, ForwardIterator2>
      mismatch(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class BinaryPredicate>
    pair<ForwardIterator1, ForwardIterator2>
      mismatch(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2,
               BinaryPredicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, InputIterator I2, Sentinel<I2> S2,}@
        @\added{class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<projected<I1, Proj1>, projected<I2, Proj2>{}> Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in1(I1), tag::in2(I2)>}@
        @\added{mismatch(I1 first1, S1 last1, I2 first2, S2 last2, Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng1, InputRange Rng2,}@
        @\added{class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<projected<iterator_t<Rng1>, Proj1>,}@
          @\added{projected<iterator_t<Rng2>, Proj2>{}> Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in1(safe_iterator_t<Rng1>),}@
                  @\added{tag::in2(safe_iterator_t<Rng2>)>}@
        @\added{mismatch(Rng1\&\& rng1, Rng2\&\& rng2, Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.equal}, equal
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2>
    constexpr bool equal(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
                         InputIterator2 first2);
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr bool equal(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
                         InputIterator2 first2, BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2>
    constexpr bool equal(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
                         InputIterator2 first2, InputIterator2 last2);
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr bool equal(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
                         InputIterator2 first2, InputIterator2 last2,
                         BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    bool equal(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class BinaryPredicate>
    bool equal(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2, BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    bool equal(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class BinaryPredicate>
    bool equal(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
               ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2,
               BinaryPredicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, InputIterator I2, Sentinel<I2> S2,}@
        @\added{class Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>, class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyComparable<I1, I2, Pred, Proj1, Proj2>}@
      @\added{bool equal(I1 first1, S1 last1, I2 first2, S2 last2,}@
                @\added{Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng1, InputRange Rng2, class Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyComparable<iterator_t<Rng1>, iterator_t<Rng2>, Pred, Proj1, Proj2>}@
      @\added{bool equal(Rng1\&\& rng1, Rng2\&\& rng2, Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.is_permutation}, is permutation
  template<class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    constexpr bool is_permutation(ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
                                  ForwardIterator2 first2);
  template<class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr bool is_permutation(ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
                                  ForwardIterator2 first2, BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    constexpr bool is_permutation(ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
                                  ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2);
  template<class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr bool is_permutation(ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
                                  ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2,
                                  BinaryPredicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, ForwardIterator I2,}@
        @\added{Sentinel<I2> S2, class Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>, class Proj1 = identity,}@
        @\added{class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyComparable<I1, I2, Pred, Proj1, Proj2>}@
      @\added{bool is_permutation(I1 first1, S1 last1, I2 first2, S2 last2,}@
                          @\added{Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                          @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@

    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng1, ForwardRange Rng2, class Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyComparable<iterator_t<Rng1>, iterator_t<Rng2>, Pred, Proj1, Proj2>}@
      @\added{bool is_permutation(Rng1\&\& rng1, Rng2\&\& rng2, Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                          @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.search}, search
  template<class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    constexpr ForwardIterator1
      search(ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
             ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2);
  template<class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr ForwardIterator1
      search(ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
             ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2,
             BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    ForwardIterator1
      search(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
             ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
             ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class BinaryPredicate>
    ForwardIterator1
      search(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
             ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
             ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2,
             BinaryPredicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, ForwardIterator I2,}@
        @\added{Sentinel<I2> S2, class Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyComparable<I1, I2, Pred, Proj1, Proj2>}@
      @\added{I1 search(I1 first1, S1 last1, I2 first2, S2 last2,}@
                @\added{Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@

    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng1, ForwardRange Rng2, class Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyComparable<iterator_t<Rng1>, iterator_t<Rng2>, Pred, Proj1, Proj2>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng1>}@
        @\added{search(Rng1\&\& rng1, Rng2\&\& rng2, Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
              @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class ForwardIterator, class Size, class T>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      search_n(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
               Size count, const T& value);
  template<class ForwardIterator, class Size, class T, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      search_n(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
               Size count, const T& value,
               BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Size, class T>
    ForwardIterator
      search_n(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
               Size count, const T& value);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Size, class T,
           class BinaryPredicate>
    ForwardIterator
      search_n(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
               ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
               Size count, const T& value,
               BinaryPredicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T,}@
        @\added{class Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyComparable<I, const T*, Pred, Proj>}@
      @\added{I search_n(I first, S last, iter_difference_t<I> count,}@
                @\added{const T\& value, Pred pred = Pred\{\},}@
                @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@

    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class T, class Pred = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyComparable<iterator_t<Rng>, const T*, Pred, Proj>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{search_n(Rng\&\& rng, iter_difference_t<iterator_t<Rng>{}> count,}@
                @\added{const T\& value, Pred pred = Pred\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  template<class ForwardIterator, class Searcher>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      search(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last, const Searcher& searcher);

  // \ref{alg.modifying.operations}, mutating sequence operations
  // \ref{alg.copy}, copy
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator>
    constexpr OutputIterator copy(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                                  OutputIterator result);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    ForwardIterator2 copy(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                          ForwardIterator1 first, ForwardIterator1 last,
                          ForwardIterator2 result);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, WeaklyIncrementable O>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{copy(I first, S last, O result);}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, WeaklyIncrementable O>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng>, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{copy(Rng\&\& rng, O result);}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class InputIterator, class Size, class OutputIterator>
    constexpr OutputIterator copy_n(InputIterator first, Size n,
                                    OutputIterator result);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class Size,
           class ForwardIterator2>
    ForwardIterator2 copy_n(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                            ForwardIterator1 first, Size n,
                            ForwardIterator2 result);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, WeaklyIncrementable O>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{copy_n(I first, iter_difference_t<I> n, O result);}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator, class Predicate>
    constexpr OutputIterator copy_if(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                                     OutputIterator result, Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class Predicate>
    ForwardIterator2 copy_if(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                             ForwardIterator1 first, ForwardIterator1 last,
                             ForwardIterator2 result, Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, WeaklyIncrementable O, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{copy_if(I first, S last, O result, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, WeaklyIncrementable O, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng>, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{copy_if(Rng\&\& rng, O result, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class BidirectionalIterator1, class BidirectionalIterator2>
    constexpr BidirectionalIterator2
      copy_backward(BidirectionalIterator1 first, BidirectionalIterator1 last,
                    BidirectionalIterator2 result);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <BidirectionalIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, BidirectionalIterator I2>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I1, I2>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I1), tag::out(I2)>}@
        @\added{copy_backward(I1 first, S1 last, I2 result);}@
    @\added{template <BidirectionalRange Rng, BidirectionalIterator I>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng>, I>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(I)>}@
        @\added{copy_backward(Rng\&\& rng, I result);}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.move}, move
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator>
    constexpr OutputIterator move(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                                  OutputIterator result);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, WeaklyIncrementable O>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyMovable<I, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{move(I first, S last, O result);}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, WeaklyIncrementable O>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyMovable<iterator_t<Rng>, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{move(Rng\&\& rng, O result);}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1,
           class ForwardIterator2>
    ForwardIterator2 move(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                          ForwardIterator1 first, ForwardIterator1 last,
                          ForwardIterator2 result);
  template<class BidirectionalIterator1, class BidirectionalIterator2>
    constexpr BidirectionalIterator2
      move_backward(BidirectionalIterator1 first, BidirectionalIterator1 last,
                    BidirectionalIterator2 result);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <BidirectionalIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, BidirectionalIterator I2>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyMovable<I1, I2>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I1), tag::out(I2)>}@
        @\added{move_backward(I1 first, S1 last, I2 result);}@
    @\added{template <BidirectionalRange Rng, BidirectionalIterator I>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyMovable<iterator_t<Rng>, I>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(I)>}@
        @\added{move_backward(Rng\&\& rng, I result);}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.swap}, swap
  template<class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    ForwardIterator2 swap_ranges(ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
                                 ForwardIterator2 first2);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    ForwardIterator2 swap_ranges(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                                 ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
                                 ForwardIterator2 first2);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, ForwardIterator I2, Sentinel<I2> S2>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlySwappable<I1, I2>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in1(I1), tag::in2(I2)>}@
        @\added{swap_ranges(I1 first1, S1 last1, I2 first2, S2 last2);}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng1, ForwardRange Rng2>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlySwappable<iterator_t<Rng1>, iterator_t<Rng2>{}>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in1(safe_iterator_t<Rng1>), tag::in2(safe_iterator_t<Rng2>)>}@
        @\added{swap_ranges(Rng1\&\& rng1, Rng2\&\& rng2);}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    void iter_swap(ForwardIterator1 a, ForwardIterator2 b);

  // \ref{alg.transform}, transform
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator, class UnaryOperation>
    constexpr OutputIterator
      transform(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                OutputIterator result, UnaryOperation op);
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2, class OutputIterator,
           class BinaryOperation>
    constexpr OutputIterator
      transform(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
                InputIterator2 first2, OutputIterator result,
                BinaryOperation binary_op);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class UnaryOperation>
    ForwardIterator2
      transform(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                ForwardIterator1 first, ForwardIterator1 last,
                ForwardIterator2 result, UnaryOperation op);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class ForwardIterator, class BinaryOperation>
    ForwardIterator
      transform(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
                ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator result,
                BinaryOperation binary_op);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, WeaklyIncrementable O,}@
        @\added{CopyConstructible F, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Writable<O, indirect_result_t<F\&, projected<I, Proj>{}>{}>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{transform(I first, S last, O result, F op, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, WeaklyIncrementable O, CopyConstructible F,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Writable<O, indirect_result_t<F\&, projected<iterator_t<R>, Proj>{}>{}>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{transform(Rng\&\& rng, O result, F op, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, InputIterator I2, Sentinel<I2> S2,}@
        @\added{WeaklyIncrementable O, CopyConstructible F, class Proj1 = identity,}@
        @\added{class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Writable<O, indirect_result_t<F\&, projected<I1, Proj1>,}@
        @\added{projected<I2, Proj2>{}>{}>}@
      @\added{tagged_tuple<tag::in1(I1), tag::in2(I2), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{transform(I1 first1, S1 last1, I2 first2, S2 last2, O result,}@
                @\added{F binary_op, Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng1, InputRange Rng2, WeaklyIncrementable O,}@
        @\added{CopyConstructible F, class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Writable<O, indirect_result_t<F\&,}@
        @\added{projected<iterator_t<Rng1>, Proj1>, projected<iterator_t<Rng2>, Proj2>{}>{}>}@
      @\added{tagged_tuple<tag::in1(safe_iterator_t<Rng1>),}@
                   @\added{tag::in2(safe_iterator_t<Rng2>),}@
                   @\added{tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{transform(Rng1\&\& rng1, Rng2\&\& rng2, O result,}@
                  @\added{F binary_op, Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.replace}, replace
  template<class ForwardIterator, class T>
    constexpr void replace(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                           const T& old_value, const T& new_value);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class T>
    void replace(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                 ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                 const T& old_value, const T& new_value);
  template<class ForwardIterator, class Predicate, class T>
    constexpr void replace_if(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                              Predicate pred, const T& new_value);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Predicate, class T>
    void replace_if(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                    ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                    Predicate pred, const T& new_value);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T1, class T2, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Writable<I, const T2\&> \&\&}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<I, Proj>, const T1*>}@
      @\added{I replace(I first, S last, const T1\& old_value, const T2\& new_value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class T1, class T2, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Writable<iterator_t<Rng>, const T2\&> \&\&}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>, const T1*>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{replace(Rng\&\& rng, const T1\& old_value, const T2\& new_value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires Writable<I, const T\&>}@
      @\added{I replace_if(I first, S last, Pred pred, const T\& new_value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class T, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires Writable<iterator_t<Rng>, const T\&>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{replace_if(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, const T\& new_value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator, class T>
    constexpr OutputIterator replace_copy(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                                          OutputIterator result,
                                          const T& old_value, const T& new_value);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2, class T>
    ForwardIterator2 replace_copy(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                                  ForwardIterator1 first, ForwardIterator1 last,
                                  ForwardIterator2 result,
                                  const T& old_value, const T& new_value);
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator, class Predicate, class T>
    constexpr OutputIterator replace_copy_if(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                                             OutputIterator result,
                                             Predicate pred, const T& new_value);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class Predicate, class T>
    ForwardIterator2 replace_copy_if(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                                     ForwardIterator1 first, ForwardIterator1 last,
                                     ForwardIterator2 result,
                                     Predicate pred, const T& new_value);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T1, class T2, OutputIterator<const T2\&> O,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I, O> \&\&}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<I, Proj>, const T1*>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{replace_copy(I first, S last, O result, const T1\& old_value, const T2\& new_value,}@
                    @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class T1, class T2, OutputIterator<const T2\&> O,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng>, O> \&\&}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>, const T1*>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{replace_copy(Rng\&\& rng, O result, const T1\& old_value, const T2\& new_value,}@
                    @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T, OutputIterator<const T\&> O,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity, IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{replace_copy_if(I first, S last, O result, Pred pred, const T\& new_value,}@
                        @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class T, OutputIterator<const T\&> O, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng>, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{replace_copy_if(Rng\&\& rng, O result, Pred pred, const T\& new_value,}@
                        @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.fill}, fill
  template<class ForwardIterator, class T>
    constexpr void fill(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last, const T& value);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class T>

           class Size, class T>
    ForwardIterator fill_n(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}

      @\added{O fill_n(O first, iter_difference_t<O> n, const T\& value);}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.generate}, generate
  template<class ForwardIterator, class Generator>
    constexpr void generate(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                            Generator gen);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Generator>
    void generate(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                  ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                  Generator gen);
  template<class OutputIterator, class Size, class Generator>
    constexpr OutputIterator generate_n(OutputIterator first, Size n, Generator gen);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Size, class Generator>
    ForwardIterator generate_n(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                               ForwardIterator first, Size n, Generator gen);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <Iterator O, Sentinel<O> S, CopyConstructible F>}@
        @\added{requires Invocable<F\&> \&\& Writable<O, invoke_result_t<F\&>{}>}@
      @\added{O generate(O first, S last, F gen);}@
    @\added{template <class Rng, CopyConstructible F>}@
        @\added{requires Invocable<F\&> \&\& OutputRange<Rng, invoke_result_t<F\&>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{generate(Rng\&\& rng, F gen);}@
    @\added{template <Iterator O, CopyConstructible F>}@
        @\added{requires Invocable<F\&> \&\& Writable<O, invoke_result_t<F\&>{}>}@
      @\added{O generate_n(O first, iter_difference_t<O> n, F gen);}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.remove}, remove
  template<class ForwardIterator, class T>
    constexpr ForwardIterator remove(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                                     const T& value);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class T>
    ForwardIterator remove(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                           ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                           const T& value);
  template<class ForwardIterator, class Predicate>
    constexpr ForwardIterator remove_if(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                                        Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Predicate>
    ForwardIterator remove_if(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                              ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                              Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Permutable<I> \&\&}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<I, Proj>, const T*>}@
      @\added{I remove(I first, S last, const T\& value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class T, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Permutable<iterator_t<Rng>{}> \&\&}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>, const T*>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{remove(Rng\&\& rng, const T\& value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires Permutable<I>}@
      @\added{I remove_if(I first, S last, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires Permutable<iterator_t<Rng>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{remove_if(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator, class T>
    constexpr OutputIterator
      remove_copy(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                  OutputIterator result, const T& value);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class T>
    ForwardIterator2
      remove_copy(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                  ForwardIterator1 first, ForwardIterator1 last,
                  ForwardIterator2 result, const T& value);
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator, class Predicate>
    constexpr OutputIterator
      remove_copy_if(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                     OutputIterator result, Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class Predicate>
    ForwardIterator2
      remove_copy_if(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                     ForwardIterator1 first, ForwardIterator1 last,
                     ForwardIterator2 result, Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, WeaklyIncrementable O, class T,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I, O> \&\&}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<I, Proj>, const T*>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{remove_copy(I first, S last, O result, const T\& value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, WeaklyIncrementable O, class T, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng>, O> \&\&}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<\added{ranges::}equal_to<>, projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>, const T*>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{remove_copy(Rng\&\& rng, O result, const T\& value, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, WeaklyIncrementable O,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity, IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{remove_copy_if(I first, S last, O result, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, WeaklyIncrementable O, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng>, O>}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{remove_copy_if(Rng\&\& rng, O result, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.unique}, unique
  template<class ForwardIterator>
    constexpr ForwardIterator unique(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last);
  template<class ForwardIterator, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr ForwardIterator unique(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                                     BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator>
    ForwardIterator unique(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                           ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class BinaryPredicate>
    ForwardIterator unique(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                           ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                           BinaryPredicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<projected<I, Proj>{}> R = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{requires Permutable<I>}@
      @\added{I unique(I first, S last, R comp = R\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> R = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{requires Permutable<iterator_t<Rng>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{unique(Rng\&\& rng, R comp = R\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator>
    constexpr OutputIterator
      unique_copy(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                  OutputIterator result);
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator, class BinaryPredicate>
    constexpr OutputIterator
      unique_copy(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                  OutputIterator result, BinaryPredicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2>
    ForwardIterator2
      unique_copy(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                  ForwardIterator1 first, ForwardIterator1 last,
                  ForwardIterator2 result);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class BinaryPredicate>
    ForwardIterator2
      unique_copy(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                  ForwardIterator1 first, ForwardIterator1 last,
                  ForwardIterator2 result, BinaryPredicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, WeaklyIncrementable O,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity, IndirectRelation<projected<I, Proj>{}> R = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I, O> \&\&}@
        @\added{(ForwardIterator<I> ||}@
        @\added{(InputIterator<O> \&\& Same<iter_value_t<I>, iter_value_t<O>{}>) ||}@
        @\added{IndirectlyCopyableStorable<I, O>)}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(I), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{unique_copy(I first, S last, O result, R comp = R\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, WeaklyIncrementable O, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectRelation<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> R = \added{ranges::}equal_to<>{}>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng>, O> \&\&}@
        @\added{(ForwardIterator<iterator_t<Rng>{}> ||}@
        @\added{(InputIterator<O> \&\& Same<iter_value_t<iterator_t<Rng>{}>, iter_value_t<O>{}>) ||}@
        @\added{IndirectlyCopyableStorable<iterator_t<Rng>, O>)}@
      @\added{tagged_pair<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{unique_copy(Rng\&\& rng, O result, R comp = R\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.reverse}, reverse

  // \ref{alg.partitions}, partitions

    constexpr bool is_partitioned(InputIterator first, InputIterator last, Predicate pred);

                        ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last, Predicate pred);

    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{bool is_partitioned(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  template<class ForwardIterator, class Predicate>
    ForwardIterator partition(ForwardIterator first,
                              ForwardIterator last,
                              Predicate pred);

    ForwardIterator partition(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                              ForwardIterator first,

                              Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@

      @\added{requires Permutable<I>}@
      @\added{I partition(I first, S last, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@

    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires Permutable<iterator_t<Rng>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{partition(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class BidirectionalIterator, class Predicate>
    BidirectionalIterator stable_partition(BidirectionalIterator first,
                                           BidirectionalIterator last,
                                           Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class BidirectionalIterator, class Predicate>
    BidirectionalIterator stable_partition(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                                           BidirectionalIterator first,
                                           BidirectionalIterator last,
                                           Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <BidirectionalIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@

      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{stable_partition(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class InputIterator, class OutputIterator1,
           class OutputIterator2, class Predicate>
    constexpr pair<OutputIterator1, OutputIterator2>
      partition_copy(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                     OutputIterator1 out_true, OutputIterator2 out_false,
                     Predicate pred);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class ForwardIterator1,
           class ForwardIterator2, class Predicate>
    pair<ForwardIterator1, ForwardIterator2>
      partition_copy(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                     ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                     ForwardIterator1 out_true, ForwardIterator2 out_false,
                     Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, WeaklyIncrementable O1, WeaklyIncrementable O2,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity, IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I, O1> \&\& IndirectlyCopyable<I, O2>}@
      @\added{tagged_tuple<tag::in(I), tag::out1(O1), tag::out2(O2)>}@
        @\added{partition_copy(I first, S last, O1 out_true, O2 out_false, Pred pred,}@
                      @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@

    @\added{template <InputRange Rng, WeaklyIncrementable O1, WeaklyIncrementable O2,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng>, O1> \&\&}@
        @\added{IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng>, O2>}@
      @\added{tagged_tuple<tag::in(safe_iterator_t<Rng>), tag::out1(O1), tag::out2(O2)>}@
        @\added{partition_copy(Rng\&\& rng, O1 out_true, O2 out_false, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class ForwardIterator, class Predicate>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      partition_point(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                      Predicate pred);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<I, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{I partition_point(I first, S last, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectUnaryPredicate<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Pred>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{partition_point(Rng\&\& rng, Pred pred, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.sorting}, sorting and related operations
  // \ref{alg.sort}, sorting
  template<class RandomAccessIterator>
    void sort(RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator last);
  template<class RandomAccessIterator, class Compare>
    void sort(RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator last,
              Compare comp);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class RandomAccessIterator>
    void sort(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
              RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator last);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class RandomAccessIterator, class Compare>
    void sort(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
              RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator last,
              Compare comp);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <RandomAccessIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Sortable<I, Comp, Proj>}@
      @\added{I sort(I first, S last, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@

    @\added{template <RandomAccessRange Rng, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Sortable<iterator_t<Rng>, Comp, Proj>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{sort(Rng\&\& rng, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  template<class RandomAccessIterator>
    void stable_sort(RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator last);
  template<class RandomAccessIterator, class Compare>
    void stable_sort(RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator last,
                     Compare comp);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class RandomAccessIterator>
    void stable_sort(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                     RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator last);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class RandomAccessIterator, class Compare>
    void stable_sort(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                     RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator last,
                     Compare comp);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <RandomAccessIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Sortable<I, Comp, Proj>}@
      @\added{I stable_sort(I first, S last, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <RandomAccessRange Rng, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Sortable<iterator_t<Rng>, Comp, Proj>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{stable_sort(Rng\&\& rng, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  template<class RandomAccessIterator>
    void partial_sort(RandomAccessIterator first,
                      RandomAccessIterator middle,
                      RandomAccessIterator last);
  template<class RandomAccessIterator, class Compare>
    void partial_sort(RandomAccessIterator first,
                      RandomAccessIterator middle,
                      RandomAccessIterator last, Compare comp);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class RandomAccessIterator>
    void partial_sort(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                      RandomAccessIterator first,
                      RandomAccessIterator middle,
                      RandomAccessIterator last);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class RandomAccessIterator, class Compare>
    void partial_sort(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                      RandomAccessIterator first,
                      RandomAccessIterator middle,
                      RandomAccessIterator last, Compare comp);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <RandomAccessIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Sortable<I, Comp, Proj>}@
      @\added{I partial_sort(I first, I middle, S last, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <RandomAccessRange Rng, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Sortable<iterator_t<Rng>, Comp, Proj>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{partial_sort(Rng\&\& rng, iterator_t<Rng> middle, Comp comp = Comp\{\},}@
                    @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class InputIterator, class RandomAccessIterator>
    RandomAccessIterator
      partial_sort_copy(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                        RandomAccessIterator result_first,
                        RandomAccessIterator result_last);
  template<class InputIterator, class RandomAccessIterator, class Compare>
    RandomAccessIterator
      partial_sort_copy(InputIterator first, InputIterator last,
                        RandomAccessIterator result_first,
                        RandomAccessIterator result_last,
                        Compare comp);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class RandomAccessIterator>
    RandomAccessIterator
      partial_sort_copy(ExecutionPolicy&& exec,  // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                        ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                        RandomAccessIterator result_first,
                        RandomAccessIterator result_last);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class RandomAccessIterator,
           class Compare>
    RandomAccessIterator
      partial_sort_copy(ExecutionPolicy&& exec,  // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                        ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                        RandomAccessIterator result_first,
                        RandomAccessIterator result_last,
                        Compare comp);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, RandomAccessIterator I2, Sentinel<I2> S2,}@
        @\added{class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>, class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<I1, I2> \&\& Sortable<I2, Comp, Proj2> \&\&}@
          @\added{IndirectStrictWeakOrder<Comp, projected<I1, Proj1>, projected<I2, Proj2>{}>}@
      @\added{I2 partial_sort_copy(I1 first, S1 last, I2 result_first, S2 result_last,}@
                           @\added{Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng1, RandomAccessRange Rng2, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires IndirectlyCopyable<iterator_t<Rng1>, iterator_t<Rng2>{}> \&\&}@
          @\added{Sortable<iterator_t<Rng2>, Comp, Proj2> \&\&}@
          @\added{IndirectStrictWeakOrder<Comp, projected<iterator_t<Rng1>, Proj1>,}@
            @\added{projected<iterator_t<Rng2>, Proj2>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng2>}@
        @\added{partial_sort_copy(Rng1\&\& rng, Rng2\&\& result_rng, Comp comp = Comp\{\},}@
                          @\added{Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class ForwardIterator>
    constexpr bool is_sorted(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last);
  template<class ForwardIterator, class Compare>
    constexpr bool is_sorted(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                             Compare comp);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator>
    bool is_sorted(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                   ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Compare>
    bool is_sorted(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                   ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                   Compare comp);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectStrictWeakOrder<projected<I, Proj>{}> Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>{}>}@
      @\added{bool is_sorted(I first, S last, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectStrictWeakOrder<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>{}>}@
      @\added{bool is_sorted(Rng\&\& rng, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@
  template<class ForwardIterator>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      is_sorted_until(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last);
  template<class ForwardIterator, class Compare>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      is_sorted_until(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                      Compare comp);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator>
    ForwardIterator
      is_sorted_until(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                      ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator, class Compare>
    ForwardIterator
      is_sorted_until(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                      ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                      Compare comp);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectStrictWeakOrder<projected<I, Proj>{}> Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>{}>}@
      @\added{I is_sorted_until(I first, S last, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectStrictWeakOrder<projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{is_sorted_until(Rng\&\& rng, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.nth.element}, Nth element
  template<class RandomAccessIterator>
    void nth_element(RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator nth,
                     RandomAccessIterator last);
  template<class RandomAccessIterator, class Compare>
    void nth_element(RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator nth,
                     RandomAccessIterator last, Compare comp);

    void nth_element(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}

    void nth_element(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
                     RandomAccessIterator first, RandomAccessIterator nth,
                     RandomAccessIterator last, Compare comp);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <RandomAccessIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Sortable<I, Comp, Proj>}@
      @\added{I nth_element(I first, I nth, S last, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <RandomAccessRange Rng, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>, class Proj = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Sortable<iterator_t<Rng>, Comp, Proj>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{nth_element(Rng\&\& rng, iterator_t<Rng> nth, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.binary.search}, binary search
  template<class ForwardIterator, class T>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      lower_bound(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                  const T& value);
  template<class ForwardIterator, class T, class Compare>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      lower_bound(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                  const T& value, Compare comp);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectStrictWeakOrder<const T*, projected<I, Proj>{}> Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>{}>}@
      @\added{I lower_bound(I first, S last, const T\& value, Comp comp = Comp\{\},}@
                    @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class T, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectStrictWeakOrder<const T*, projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{lower_bound(Rng\&\& rng, const T\& value, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  template<class ForwardIterator, class T>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      upper_bound(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                  const T& value);
  template<class ForwardIterator, class T, class Compare>
    constexpr ForwardIterator
      upper_bound(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                  const T& value, Compare comp);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T, class Proj = identity,}@

      @\added{I upper_bound(I first, S last, const T\& value, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class T, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectStrictWeakOrder<const T*, projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>{}>}@
      @\added{safe_iterator_t<Rng>}@
        @\added{upper_bound(Rng\&\& rng, const T\& value, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  template<class ForwardIterator, class T>
    constexpr pair<ForwardIterator, ForwardIterator>
      equal_range(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                  const T& value);
  template<class ForwardIterator, class T, class Compare>
    constexpr pair<ForwardIterator, ForwardIterator>
      equal_range(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                  const T& value, Compare comp);

        @\added{equal_range(I first, S last, const T\& value, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class T, class Proj = identity,}@

                  @\added{tag::end(safe_iterator_t<Rng>)>}@
        @\added{equal_range(Rng\&\& rng, const T\& value, Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

    constexpr bool
      binary_search(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                    const T& value);

    constexpr bool
      binary_search(ForwardIterator first, ForwardIterator last,
                    const T& value, Compare comp);

    @\added{template <ForwardIterator I, Sentinel<I> S, class T, class Proj = identity,}@

      @\added{bool binary_search(I first, S last, const T\& value, Comp comp = Comp\{\},}@
                         @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
    @\added{template <ForwardRange Rng, class T, class Proj = identity,}@
        @\added{IndirectStrictWeakOrder<const T*, projected<iterator_t<Rng>, Proj>{}> Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>{}>}@
      @\added{bool binary_search(Rng\&\& rng, const T\& value, Comp comp = Comp\{\},}@
                         @\added{Proj proj = Proj\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  // \ref{alg.merge}, merge
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2, class OutputIterator>
    constexpr OutputIterator
      merge(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
            InputIterator2 first2, InputIterator2 last2,
            OutputIterator result);
  template<class InputIterator1, class InputIterator2, class OutputIterator,
           class Compare>
    constexpr OutputIterator
      merge(InputIterator1 first1, InputIterator1 last1,
            InputIterator2 first2, InputIterator2 last2,
            OutputIterator result, Compare comp);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class ForwardIterator>
    ForwardIterator
      merge(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
            ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
            ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2,
            ForwardIterator result);
  template<class ExecutionPolicy, class ForwardIterator1, class ForwardIterator2,
           class ForwardIterator, class Compare>
    ForwardIterator
      merge(ExecutionPolicy&& exec, // see \ref{algorithms.parallel.overloads}
            ForwardIterator1 first1, ForwardIterator1 last1,
            ForwardIterator2 first2, ForwardIterator2 last2,
            ForwardIterator result, Compare comp);
  @\added{namespace ranges \{}@
    @\added{template <InputIterator I1, Sentinel<I1> S1, InputIterator I2, Sentinel<I2> S2,}@
        @\added{WeaklyIncrementable O, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>, class Proj1 = identity,}@
        @\added{class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Mergeable<I1, I2, O, Comp, Proj1, Proj2>}@
      @\added{tagged_tuple<tag::in1(I1), tag::in2(I2), tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{merge(I1 first1, S1 last1, I2 first2, S2 last2, O result,}@
              @\added{Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
    @\added{template <InputRange Rng1, InputRange Rng2, WeaklyIncrementable O, class Comp = \added{ranges::}less<>,}@
        @\added{class Proj1 = identity, class Proj2 = identity>}@
      @\added{requires Mergeable<iterator_t<Rng1>, iterator_t<Rng2>, O, Comp, Proj1, Proj2>}@
      @\added{tagged_tuple<tag::in1(safe_iterator_t<Rng1>),}@
                   @\added{tag::in2(safe_iterator_t<Rng2>),}@
                   @\added{tag::out(O)>}@
        @\added{merge(Rng1\&\& rng1, Rng2\&\& rng2, O result,}@
              @\added{Comp comp = Comp\{\}, Proj1 proj1 = Proj1\{\}, Proj2 proj2 = Proj2\{\});}@
  @\added{\}}@

  template<class BidirectionalIterator>
    void inplace_merge(BidirectionalIterator first,
                       BidirectionalIterator middle,
                       BidirectionalIterator last);
  template<class BidirectionalIterator, class Compare>
    void inplace_merge(BidirectionalIterator first,
                       BidirectionalIterator middle,
                       BidirectionalIterator last, Compare comp);
